Initiative 1.2: Decision-Making Architecture Redesign

Objective

Implement clear decision rights framework to improve decision-making effectiveness from 2/5 to 3/5

Strategic Rationale

  • 4 executives managing 170 employees creates severe bottlenecks
  • Decision-making effectiveness rated 2/5 (below 10th percentile)
  • 270-day sales cycle partly driven by decision delays
  • 24-hour response time linked to escalation bottlenecks
  • Foundation for all subsequent organizational improvements

Implementation Details

ElementSpecification
OwnerCEO (Primary), with COO/CHRO support
TimelineWeeks 2-10
Investment$25,000 - $50,000 (external facilitation, tools)

Initiative 1.3: Customer Response Time Quick Win

Objective

Reduce average customer response time from 24 hours to 12 hours within 90 days

Strategic Rationale

  • 24-hour response time is 6x slower than industry P90 (4 hours)
  • Threatens 98% retention rate ($23.5M annual revenue at risk)
  • Quick win that demonstrates improvement capability
  • Foundation for customer experience excellence
  • Links to technology infrastructure investment (5/5) underutilization

Implementation Details

ElementSpecification
OwnerCOO (Primary), Customer Success Lead
TimelineWeeks 1-10
Investment$65,000 - $100,000

Initiative 1.4: Advisory Board Formation Launch

Objective

Identify and begin recruiting 3-5 advisory board members to address governance gap

Strategic Rationale

  • No advisory board exists (governance gap identified across all analyses)
  • Board oversight rated 2/5 (below 10th percentile)
  • Advisory expertise needed for capital strategy, growth execution, exit planning
  • External perspective on decision-making and strategy
  • Builds credibility with customers, employees, potential acquirers

Implementation Details

ElementSpecification
OwnerCEO (Primary)
TimelineWeeks 4-12 (formation continues into Phase 2)
Investment$10,000 - $20,000 (Phase 1 identification and initial engagement)

Initiative 1.5: Financial Data Quality Remediation

Objective

Remediate identified financial data quality issues to support credit facility and management decision-making

Strategic Rationale

  • Financial analysis revealed data inconsistencies (e.g., $3.5M monthly expenses reported vs. $24M annual revenue)
  • Accurate financial data required for credit facility due diligence
  • Foundation for improved financial planning and forecasting
  • Supports cash flow management and growth investment decisions

Implementation Details

ElementSpecification
OwnerCFO (Primary), Controller/Finance Lead
TimelineWeeks 1-8
Investment$25,000 - $50,000 (consulting support, system improvements)

Action Steps

WeekActivityDeliverableOwner
1-2Audit current financial reporting for inconsistenciesData quality assessmentCFO
1-2Reconcile monthly expense data with annual totalsReconciliation reportController
2-3Document total debt and liability positionComplete debt scheduleCFO
2-4Implement accurate monthly cash flow trackingCash flow statement processController
3-5Calculate and document cash runway scenariosCash runway analysisCFO
4-6Establish standardized monthly financial packageFinancial reporting templateCFO
5-8Implement financial dashboard for key metricsDashboard deploymentFinance/IT

Success Metrics

MetricTargetMeasurement
Data discrepancy rate<2% variance month-over-monthReconciliation review
Financial close cycleâ‰¤10 business daysCalendar tracking
Key metrics tracked100% of critical financial KPIsDashboard coverage
Credit facility data room complete100% documentationLender feedback

Initiative 1.6: Sales Win/Loss Analysis Program

Objective

Conduct structured analysis of recent wins and losses to identify conversion improvement levers

Strategic Rationale

  • 10% close rate is below 10th percentile (vs. 25% benchmark)
  • Each 5-point improvement = ~$1.5M additional annual revenue
  • Root cause understanding required before sales investment
  • Addresses competitive differentiation clarity gap (3/5)

Implementation Details

ElementSpecification
OwnerVP Sales/CRO (Primary), CEO (Sponsor)
TimelineWeeks 4-12
Investment$20,000 - $35,000

Action Steps

WeekActivityDeliverableOwner
4-5Identify last 20 closed-won and 20 closed-lost opportunitiesAnalysis sampleSales Ops
5-6Develop interview protocol (customer and internal perspectives)Interview guideSales/External
6-9Conduct win/loss interviews (10 customer, 40 internal)Interview transcriptsExternal consultant
9-10Analyze patterns and synthesize findingsWin/loss analysis reportExternal consultant
10-11Identify top 3 deal-breaking factors and top 3 success driversInsight summaryVP Sales
11-12Develop action plan for sales enablement improvementsSales improvement roadmapVP Sales

Success Metrics

MetricTargetMeasurement
Interviews completed40+ totalInterview log
Actionable insights identified5+ major insightsAnalysis report
Sales team alignment100% review of findingsTeam meeting attendance
Improvement actions defined8-10 specific actionsRoadmap document

Phase 2: Stabilization (3-6 Months)

Strategic Intent

Phase 2 builds core capabilities and processes that enable sustainable growth. With the foundation established in Phase 1 (capital secured, decision framework operational, quick wins demonstrated), Phase 2 focuses on systematic improvement of sales efficiency, margin structure, and organizational health.

Initiative 2.1: Sales Conversion Improvement Program

Objective

Improve close rate from 10% to 14% and reduce sales cycle from 270 to 240 days

Strategic Rationale

  • Win/loss analysis from Phase 1 provides foundation
  • Each 4-point improvement = ~$1.2M additional revenue
  • Sales velocity is primary growth constraint after capital
  • Competitive differentiation clarity (3/5) must improve

Implementation Details

ElementSpecification
OwnerVP Sales/CRO (Primary), CEO (Sponsor)
TimelineMonths 4-6
Investment$100,000 - $150,000

Initiative 2.2: Gross Margin Improvement Program

Objective

Improve gross profit margin from 32% to 34% through pricing and operational efficiency

Strategic Rationale

  • 32% GPM is below 10th percentile (vs. 42% benchmark)
  • Each 1% improvement = $240K additional gross profit
  • Margin improvement funds future growth investments
  • 50% equipment utilization suggests efficiency opportunities

Phase 3: Growth (6-12 Months)

Strategic Intent

Phase 3 executes strategic initiatives that drive measurable growth outcomes. With foundations stabilized and core capabilities built, Phase 3 focuses on scaling the business toward the 20% growth target through pricing optimization, technology activation, leadership development, and market expansion.

Objective

Implement value-based pricing to achieve 3-5% average price increase

Strategic Rationale

  • $1M LTV and 98% retention support premium positioning
  • Direct margin improvement with minimal cost
  • Each 1% price increase = ~$240K additional gross profit

â€¢ Revenue growth: 15-16% (vs. 20%)

â€¢ All other targets: Moderated proportionally

Change Management Principles

TRANSFORMATION CHANGE MANAGEMENT FRAMEWORK
â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

GUIDING PRINCIPLES:

1. TRANSPARENCY
   â€¢ Share the "why" behind changes
   â€¢ Communicate progress honestly (wins AND challenges)
   â€¢ Make metrics visible and accessible

2. INVOLVEMENT
   â€¢ Include employees in solution design where possible
   â€¢ Create feedback channels
   â€¢ Recognize contributions at all levels

3. SUPPORT
   â€¢ Provide training and resources
   â€¢ Allow time for adaptation
   â€¢ Acknowledge difficulty of change

4. CONSISTENCY
   â€¢ Leadership walks the talk
   â€¢ Apply changes fairly across organization
   â€¢ Follow through on commitments

5. CELEBRATION
   â€¢ Recognize milestone achievements
   â€¢ Celebrate individual and team contributions
   â€¢ Connect progress to organizational purpose

Conclusion

Transformation Readiness Assessment

EWM Global possesses the fundamental building blocks for a successful transformation:

âœ“ Clear strategic intent â€” 20% growth target with documented exit/growth plans
âœ“ Strong foundation â€” Exceptional customer retention, IT infrastructure, domain expertise
âœ“ Motivated leadership â€” Recognition of gaps and desire to address them
âœ“ Sufficient scale â€” $24M revenue provides investment capacity
âœ“ Market opportunity â€” 10% share with room for expansion

The 18-month roadmap addresses the critical constraints identified across all 10 Phase 1 analyses:

  1. Financial constraints resolved through credit facility and margin improvement
  2. Governance gaps closed through advisory board and decision framework
  3. Sales inefficiency transformed through systematic enablement and process improvement
  4. Cultural weakness addressed through diagnostic, values, and sustained change
  5. Technology underutilization activated through automation and adoption programs

Final Recommendation

Proceed with full transformation implementation beginning immediately.

The investment of $1.8M - $2.5M over 18 months (7-10% of cumulative revenue) is justified by:

  • Expected ROI of 180-280%
  • Payback period of approximately 11 months
  • Protection of $23.5M+ annual retention revenue
  • Achievement of 20% growth target
  • Preservation of strategic optionality (exit or continued growth)

The alternativeâ€”maintaining status quoâ€”carries higher risk:

  • Growth constrained to 12-15%
  • Competitive position erosion
  • Talent retention challenges
  • Strategic options limited

The time to act is now. Begin Phase 1 immediately with capital facility pursuit and decision framework implementation. Each month of delay increases risk and extends time to outcomes.
